NauSYS API V6 Home
   Expand all Collapse all
 Implementation guidelines
 Requirements
 A local database on your server needs to be created. This database is used to store all catalogue information which you
 receive from NauSYS server through API.
 Your local database will be populated with the catalogue data from the API. Catalogue data is the main dictionary of primary
 data used in other complex structures like YachtReservation.
 Your local database with catalogue data is preferred to be synchronised once per day during night hours after 01:00 AM
 (GMT+1)
 It is recommended to make synchronisation of occupancy more often, like once per hour or every few hours.
 You are free to manipulate data structures on your side as needed for your purposes.
 API calls to NauSYS must be executed sequentially (next after the previous finishes), this means one per one and not
 multiple requests at the same time (parallel multi threads are not allowed)
 Functional service groups
 NauSYS web services are divided into five groups:
 Catalogue - used to pull all information needed to make mappings between NauSYS and your system.
 Yacht reservation - used to get yours bookings/options or to make enquiry which yacht is available in certain period or to
 get all occupancy list of fleets.
 Booking - used to make new option/booking or cancel existing ones.
 Crew list - used to receive existing information about crewlist on the reservation or to make an update on crewlist like
 adding passengers or change data.
 Sales actions - used to receive information about special actions like ten days charter, Wednesday to Wednesday charter or
 short periods (less than a week long charters) or any normal action like last minute or early booking offers.
 Implementation scenarios
 There are several different implementation scenarios based on your functional requirements during the implementation. Scenarios
 are different by the level of implementation and complexity. Therefore, we differ three scenarios:
 Basic implementation is the most dependant type of implementation because it is relying completely on NauSYS
 Advanced implementation is less dependant comparing to Basic implementation, but still requires constant interaction with
 NauSYS to work properly
 Full implementation is almost independant 
These scenarios depend on the desired level independence and client's needs.
 In all scenarios it is mandatory to make copy of all catalogue data in your local database. This will make your
 implementation and further use of the data much more easier.
 Impementation scenario Basic Advanced Full

 Using the yacht pictures endpoint retrieves images at their
 original size, but it is possible to select an image size by using
 additional "h" and/or "w" parameters.
 e.g. https://ws.nausys.com/CBMS-external/rest/yacht/10315
 2/pictures/main.jpg?w=600
 Only responses for agency request will have fields
 maxDiscountFromCommission and agencyDiscountType
 ("Client price" & "Agency commission")

Yacht reservation
 All reservations
 Params Values
 Description: Provides all reservations in given period made by this agency
 (or charter company depending on credentials).
 Consumes: JSON (content type: application/json)
 Produces: JSON (content type: application/json)
 URL: https://ws.nausys.com/CBMS-external/rest/yachtReservation/
 v6/reservations
 Request method: POST
 Request structure: RestYachtReservationsRequest
 Response structure: RestYachtReservationList
 Example
 URL: https://ws.nausys.com/CBMS-external/rest/yachtReservation/v6/reservations
 POST param:
 Definition
 Field Type Description
 credentials RestAuthentication 
periodFrom Date min check-in date (ignored if reservation
 ids sent)
 periodTo Date max check-in date (ignored if
 reservation ids sent)
 endDateFrom Date min check-out date (ignored if
 reservation ids sent)
 endDateTo Date max check-out date (ignored if
 reservation ids sent)
 includeWaitingOptions Boolean Optional parameter. Used to display
 waiting options. true or false.
 reservations Array of Long Reservation IDs
 modifyTimeFrom DateTime1 min modify time (ignored if reservation
 ids sent)
 modifyTimeTo DateTime1 max modify time (ignored if reservation
 ids sent)
NauSYS API Documentation v6
 ...  – The fastest growing Booking System in the World ... NauSYS
 displayCurrency String Optional parameter (defaults to
 "DEFAULT")
 For charter company login possible
 values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to charter
 company)
 For agency login possible values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to agency)
 "COMPANY" (return amounts in currency
 in which the agency pays to charter
 company)
 Important notice for agency login:
 Selection of displayCurrency affects
 which payment plans and payments will
 be returned in the response.
 If a paid agency selects "CLIENT" or
 "DEFAULT" displayCurrency, payments
 plans and payments from client towards
 agency will be returned.
 If an agency selects "COMPANY"
 displayCurrency, payments plans and
 payments from agency towards charter
 company will be returned.
 Otherwise no payment plans and
 payments will be returned.
 Example
 {    
   "credentials": {        
       "username": "xxx@xxxxx",        
       "password": "xxxxxxxxx"     
   },    
  "reservations":[1001552,1001553,1001555]
 }
 
or
 
{    
   "credentials": {        
       "username": "xxx@xxxxx",        
       "password": "xxxxxxxxx"     
   },    
  "periodFrom":"23.05.2013",    
  "periodFrom":"23.05.2013",    
NauSYS API Documentation v6
  "periodTo":"23.05.2013"
 }
 or
 {    
}
   "credentials": {        
       "username": "xxx@xxxxx",        
       "password": "xxxxxxxxx"     
   },    
  "endDateFrom":"23.05.2022",    
  "endDateTo":"23.05.2022"
 or
 {    
}
   "credentials": {        
       "username": "xxx@xxxxx",        
       "password": "xxxxxxxxx"     },    
  "periodFrom":"09.03.2019",    
  "periodTo":"16.03.2019",
  "includeWaitingOptions": true

Data Types
 Name Pattern Note
 Date dd.MM.yyyy Date without time
 DateTime1 dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm Date with time without seconds
 DateTime2 dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm:ss Date with time with seconds
 Time1 HH:mm Time without seconds
 Time2 HH:mm:ss Time with seconds
 Number ###0 Integer or Long
 Decimal ###0.00 Decimal number
 Discount
 Definition
 Field Type Description Possible values
 level String discount level 1 - owners discount
 2 - discount from charter
 company
 name String name of discount 
type String discount type PERCENTAGE - discount in per
 % centages
 AMOUNT - absolute discount
 amount in invoicing currency
 amount String amount of discount amount of discount in
 invoicing currency
 altamount String total discount amount amount of discount in home
 currency (altcurrency)
 Example
 <discount level="1" name="Rani buking" type="PERCENTAGE" amount="10.00" altamount="2534.55"/>

 RestCabinPriceListPrice
 Definition
 Field
 price1
 price2
 price3
 Type
 String 
String
 Description
 only for cabinType: "DOUBLE", "SPLIT",
 "BUNK", "DOUBLE_PLUS_SINGLE"
 String
 Calculation explanation:
 price1 - price for 1 person per person
 price2 - price for 2 people per person
 price3 - price for 3 people per person
 i.e. price for DOUBLE_PLUS_SINGLE cabin for 2 people = price2 * 2

 RestCabinReservation
 Field Type Description
 id Long Official reservation number
 uuid String Security code for web service actions on
 this reservation. 
NOTE: If the important data is changed
 on the reservation, the security code is
 changed also.
 reservationStatus String Status of the reservation:
 INFO - just an offer. Doesn't block the
 yacht in that period, 
OPTION, RESERVATION - fix booking,
 STORNO - cancelled option or booking
 packageId Long 
waitingForOption Boolean 
baseFromId Long Charter base id of the embarkment base
 (to see list of all bases call All charter
 ) bases service
 baseToId Long Charter base id of the arrival base (to see
 list of all bases call All charter bases
 ) service
 locationFromId Long Location id of the embarkment base (to
 see list of all locations call All locations
 ) service
 locationToId Long Location id of the arrival base (to see list
 of all locations call ) All locations service
 periodFrom DateTime1 Period from with check in date (date
 format is dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm)
 periodTo DateTime1 Period to with check out date (date
 format is dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm)
 optionTill String Option valid till (dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm).
 Only if status is OPTION.
 agency String Name of the agency
 agencyVATID String VAT ID of the agency
 client RestClient Info about the client.

 RestCabinReservationInfoRequest
 Field Type Description
 credentials RestAuthentication 
client RestClient 
packageId Long 
periodFrom Date 
periodTo Date 
onlinePayment Boolean This parameter is TRUE only when info
 request is created for online booking
 payment, otherwise is FALSE
 promoCode String 
numberOfPayments Integer 
paymentCurrency String 
restCabins Array of RestCabinRequest 
displayCurrency String optional parameter (defaults to
 "DEFAULT")
 For charter company login possible
 values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to charter
 company)
 For agency login possible values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to agency)
 "COMPANY" (return amounts in currency
 in which the agency pays to charter
 company)
 proposal boolean Informational data of the booking
 without ID and UUID
 and reservationStatus will be "PROPOSAL"
 and it won't be saved in database.
 agencyId Long Used only in case you are Fleet operator,
 for agencies this field is ignored
 promoCode String 
additionalDiscountItem RestAdditionalDiscountItem available only for Opt charter companies. 
ional.
 overrideClientData Boolean If client already exist gives possibility to
 override his personal information.

 when field needs to be updated to "null"
 value) otherwise, only received fields are
 updated, other are left unchanged

 RestFreeYachtsRequest
 Definition
 Field Type Description
 credentials RestAuthentication 
periodFrom Date Dates passed in the request need to
 follow booking constraints for a boat.
 Booking constraint rules can be found in 
 under  which is RestYacht checkInPeriods
 an array of . RestYachtCheckInPeriod
 e.g. Most of the boats in the system are
 bookable from Saturday to Saturday
 (SAT-SAT) so the request dates for one
 week booking would need to correspond
 to two next consecutive Saturdays.
 periodTo Date Dates passed in the request need to
 follow booking constraints for a boat.
 Booking constraint rules can be found in 
 under  which is RestYacht checkInPeriods
 an array of . RestYachtCheckInPeriod
 e.g. Most of the boats in the system are
 bookable from Saturday to Saturday
 (SAT-SAT) so the request dates for one
 week booking would need to correspond
 to two next consecutive Saturdays.
 priceFrom Number 
priceTo Number 
yachts Array of Long Contains yachts id
 orderby Number 1 - base 2 - price 3 - yacht length 
4 - yacht cabins 5 - yacht build year
 desc Number 0 - ascending 1 - descending
 ignoreAvailability Boolean true or false
 periods Array of Period Used to send multiple periods in one
 request instead of sending multiple
 requests with a single period. When
 used,  and  are periodFrom periodTo
 ignored
 includeExtendedDataSet Boolean Flag for export payment plans in
 response. Use true or false. *this flag is
 deprecated please use extendedDataSet
NauSYS API Documentation v6
 ...  – The fastest growing Booking System in the World ... NauSYS
 extendedDataSet String List of extended data types separated by
 comma. Possible types: PAYMENT_PLAN,
 OBLIGATORY_SERVICES,
 ADDITIONAL_EXTRAS.
 When requesting , OBLIGATORY_SERVICES
 they will be exported only if one yacht and
 one period are requested, otherwise it will be
 ignored
 When requesting with parameter
 "extendedDataSet":
 "ADDITIONAL_EXTRAS" without any
 serviceIDs or equipmentIDs, you will get
 all additional extras possible for that
 period. Those additional extras  b will not
 e added into the total price with extras.
 Only obligatory extras will be included in
 the total price with extras. Returned
 extras IDs will be the ones form seasonS
 of the boat, and  use pecificData you can
 them in Create info requests.
 When requesting with parameter
 "extendedDataSet":
 "ADDITIONAL_EXTRAS" with serviceIDs or
 equipmentIDs included, you will get only
 those extras in the response and they wil
 included in the total price with l be
 extras. Returned extras IDs are virtual ca
 be used in subsequent Create info n not
 requests.
 When requesting without the
 "extendedDataSet":
 "ADDITIONAL_EXTRAS" parameter, you wi
 get any additional extras in the ll not
 response.
 ignoreOptions Boolean When true, result will include periods
 under options. Can be used to place
 waiting options
 serviceIDs Array of Long When extendedDataSet contains
 ADDITIONAL_EXTRAS, use this parameter
 to specify extra services you want
 included in the price. It is required to
 specify an array of extra IDs (  ) serviceId
 found in seasonSpecificData of the boat
 equipmentIDs Array of Long When extendedDataSet contains
 ADDITIONAL_EXTRAS, use this parameter
 to specify extra equipment you want
 included in the price. It is required to
 specify an array of extra IDs ( equipmentI
 ) found in seasonSpecificData of the d
 boat
 currency String currency in form EUR,HRK,USD etc...
 *includeExtendedDataSet is deprecated please use extendedDataSet.

 priceMeasureId
 Type
 Long 
Number 
String
 String 
Long
 Description
 deprecated
 Used to fetch equipment name.

 equipment
 RestInternationalText 
Long
 ... 
NauSYS
 Relates to Catalogue endpoint All price
 measures
 – The fastest growing Booking System in the World ...
NauSYS API Documentation v6
 ...  – The fastest growing Booking System in the World ... NauSYS
 calculationType String Values: SEPARATE_PAYMENT,
 ADVANCE_PAYMENT
 condition RestInternationalText 
amount String currency: 2 decimal places, percentage:
 4 decimal places
 amountIsPercentage Boolean 
percentageCalculationType String Values: PRICELIST_PRICE, CLIENT_PRICE,
 AGENCY_PRICE, DAILY_PRICE
 ,PRICELIST_PRICE_WITHOUT_VAT
 validForBases Array of Long baseFrom of the current reservation (if
 empty, applies to all bases)
 minimumPrice String minimum price for this equipment item
 validPeriodFrom String start date of the period the equipment is
 available. Date format (dd.MM.yyyy)
 validPeriodTo String end date of the period the equipment is
 available. Date format (dd.MM.yyyy)
 minDuration Integer Defines conditional availability
 of equipment in relation to booking
 duration in days. Reservation duration
 must fall between these two values
 for equipment to be available for usage.
 maxDuration Integer
 vatInPrice String Defines if the prices include or exclude
 VAT for fields: amount, minimumPrice

 id Long Option ID. Can be fetched from All

 ) or from  respons options / createOption
 e.
 uuid String Security code for web service actions on
 this reservation. Can be fetched from All
 endpoint ( options /yachtReservation/v6
 ) or from  response. options / createOption
 payment RestPayment 
displayCurrency String optional parameter (defaults to
 "DEFAULT")
 For charter company login possible
 values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to charter
 company)
 For agency login possible values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to agency)
 "COMPANY" (return amounts in currency
 in which the agency pays to charter
 company)
 Important notice for agency login:
 Selection of displayCurrency affects
 which payment plans and payments will
 be returned in the response.
 If a paid agency selects "CLIENT" or
 "DEFAULT" displayCurrency, payments
 plans and payments from client towards
 agency will be returned.
 If an agency selects "COMPANY"
 displayCurrency, payments plans and
 payments from agency towards charter
 company will be returned.
 Otherwise no payment plans and
 payments will be returned.

 rejectedUrl String Redirect to company site upon error with
 payment
 displayCurrency String Optional parameter (defaults to
 "DEFAULT")
 For charter company login possible
 values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to charter
 company)
 For agency login possible values are:
 "DEFAULT" (returns amounts in default
 reservation currency)
 "CLIENT" (returns amounts in currency in
 which the client should pay to agency)
 "COMPANY" (return amounts in currency
 in which the agency pays to charter
 company)
 Important notice for agency login:
 Selection of displayCurrency affects
 which payment plans and payments will
 be returned in the response.
 If a paid agency selects "CLIENT" or
 "DEFAULT" displayCurrency, payments
 plans and payments from client towards
 agency will be returned.
 If an agency selects "COMPANY"
 displayCurrency, payments plans and
 payments from agency towards charter
 company will be returned.
 Otherwise no payment plans and
 payments will be returned.
